					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) -- (1.5,0) -- (1.5,{1.5*tan(45)});
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (0,0) -- (1.5,{1.5*tan(45)});
				\draw[thick] (0.3,0) arc (0:45:0.3);
				\node at (0.5,0.2) {$\alpha$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			% Правый рисунок
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) -- (0:1.5) arc (0:135:1.5) -- cycle;
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (0,0) -- (135:1.5);
				\draw[thick] (0.3,0) arc (0:135:0.3);
				\node at (0.3,0.4) {$n\alpha$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			% Стрелка между рисунками
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
			
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Чтобы отображение было взаимооднозначным необходимо, чтобы $ 0 < \alpha < \dfrac{2\pi}{n}. $\\
	$w = z^n \text{--- конформно в $D_z$, где} \ D_z = \{ z \in \Cm : \beta < \arg z < \beta + \dfrac{2\pi}{n}\} $\\
	
	Рассмотрим обратное отображение $f(z) = z^\frac{1}{n} \text{ --- $n$-значная функция.}$\\
	На $\widetilde D = \Cm \setminus \{z \in \Cm: \operatorname{Im} z = 0,\  \operatorname{Re}z \geqslant 0 \}$ можно выделить $n$ однозначных ветвей.
	\[ f_k(z) = \sqrt[n]{|z|} e^\frac{i(\arg z + 2 \pi k)}{n},\ k = 0, 1, \ldots, n-1 \]
	$w = f_0(z)$ --- конформно на $\widetilde{D}$
	\newpage
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\clip (-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5) % вся плоскость
					(0, -0.05) rectangle (1.5, 0.05); % луч (вычитается)
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) -- (0:1.5) arc (0:135:1.5) -- cycle;
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (0,0) -- (135:1.5);
				\draw[thick] (0.3,0) arc (0:135:0.3);
				\node at (0.4,0.5) {$\dfrac{2\pi}{n}$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			% Стрелка между рисунками
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
			
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\subsection{Отображения, задаваемые функциями $f(z) = e^z$, $f(z) = \operatorname{Ln}(z)$}
	\subsubsection{Функция $ f(z) = e^z $}
	Её производная $f'(z) = e^z \neq 0, \ \forall z \in \Cm \Rightarrow f(z) \in \mathcal{A}(\Cm)$, она конформна на $\Cm$.\\
	$e^z = e^{x + iy} \Rightarrow |e^z| = e^x$\\
	$\forall z \in \Cm \Rightarrow e^z = e^{z + 2\pi i},\ T = 2\pi i$ --- основной период\\
	Уравнение $e^z = 0$ не имеет решений.
	\[ D = \{z \in \Cm :\ 0 < \operatorname{Im}z < 2\pi\} \text{ --- область конформности.} \]
	(Любая полоса шириной $ 2\pi $ является облостью конформности.)
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			% Левый рисунок
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (-1.5, 1) -- (1.5,1);
				
				\fill[black] (0,1) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$2\pi i$};
				\node at (0.6,-0.15) {$\Gamma_1$};
				\node at (0.6,1.15) {$\Gamma_2$};
				\node at (-0.15,0.5) {$\Gamma_3$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			% Правый рисунок
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\begin{scope}
					\clip (-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5) % вся плоскость
					(0, -0.05) rectangle (1.5, 0.05); % луч (вычитается)
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			% Стрелка между рисунками
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
			
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Парметризуем границы этой области:
	$ \begin{cases}
		\Gamma_1: z = x,\ x \in \R \Rightarrow w = e^x\\
		\Gamma_2: z = x + 2 \pi i,\ x \in \R \Rightarrow w = e^x\\
		\Gamma_3: z = x + \pi i,\ x \in \R \Rightarrow w = -e^x
	\end{cases} $
	\[ D_w = \{ w \in \Cm :\ 0 < \arg w < 2\pi \} \]
	\newpage
	\subsection*{Примеры}
	\noindent\textbf{1)} $ D_z = \{z \in \Cm :\ 0 \leqslant \operatorname{Im}z \leqslant 2\pi,\ \operatorname{Re}z \leqslant 0 \} $
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				% Левый рисунок
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (0,1);
					\end{scope}
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\draw (-1.5, 1) -- (0,1);
					\node at (-0.6,-0.15) {$\Gamma_1$};
					\node at (-0.6,1.15) {$\Gamma_3$};
					\node at (0.15,0.5) {$\Gamma_2$};
					\fill[black] (0,1) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$2\pi i$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				% Правый рисунок
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
						(0,0) circle (0.75)
						(0,-0.05) rectangle (0.75,0.05);
					\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (0,0) circle (0.75);
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				% Стрелка между рисунками
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	$ \begin{cases}
		\Gamma_1: z = x,\ x \leqslant 0 \Rightarrow w = e^x \\
		\Gamma_2: z = yi,\  0 \leqslant y \leqslant 2\pi \Rightarrow w = e^{iy}\\
		\Gamma_3: z = x + 2\pi i,\ x \leqslant 0 \Rightarrow w = e^x
	\end{cases} $
	\[ D_w = \{ w \in \Cm: |w| < 1\} \setminus \{ w \in \Cm: \operatorname{Im} w = 0,\ 0 \leqslant \operatorname{Re} w \leqslant 1 \} \]
	\noindent\textbf{2)} $ D_z = \{z \in \Cm :\ 0 \leqslant \operatorname{Im}z \leqslant 2\pi,\ \operatorname{Re}z \geqslant 0 \} $
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				% Левый рисунок
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.5,1);
					\end{scope}
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\draw (0, 1) -- (1.5,1);
					\node at (0.6,-0.15) {$\Gamma_1$};
					\node at (0.6,1.15) {$\Gamma_3$};
					\node at (-0.15,0.5) {$\Gamma_2$};
					\fill[black] (0,1) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$2\pi i$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				% Правый рисунок
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]

					\end{scope}
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};

					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				% Стрелка между рисунками
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Знаем, что вся полоса перейдет на плоскость с разрезом. Выше увидили, что левая половина перешла на круг с разрезом, а значит правая полоса перейдет во внешность окружности с разрезом.
	\[ D_w = \{ w \in \Cm: |w| > 1\} \setminus \{ w \in \Cm: \operatorname{Im} w = 0,\ \operatorname{Re} w \geqslant 1 \} \]\newpage
	\noindent\textbf{3)} Аналогичные примеры с более тонкой полоской.
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				% Левый рисунок
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]

					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\draw (-1.5, 1) -- (1.5,1);
					%\node at (0.6,-0.15) {$\Gamma_1$};

					\fill[black] (0,1) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$\pi i$};

				\end{scope}
				% Правый рисунок
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\end{scope}
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					%\node at (0.6,-0.15) {$\Gamma_1$};
					%\node at (0.6,1.15) {$\Gamma_3$};
					%\node at (-0.15,0.5) {$\Gamma_2$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				% Стрелка между рисунками
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\begin{center}

	\newpage
	\subsubsection{Функция $ f(z) = \operatorname{Ln}z $}
	\noindent
	\[ \operatorname{Ln}z = \ln{|z|} + i(\arg z +2\pi k)\text{ --- бесконечно-значная функция} \]
	\noindent
	$w = f_0(z)=\ln z=\ln{|z|} + i \arg z $ --- Главная ветвь.(Оно конформно в $ D_z $)\\
	$D_z = \Cm \setminus \{z \in \Cm: \operatorname{Im}z = 0,\ \operatorname{Re}z \geqslant 0 \}$
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\clip (-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5) % вся плоскость
					(0, -0.05) rectangle (1.5, 0.05); % луч (вычитается)
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}

			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\[ D_w= \{ w \in \Cm : 0 < \operatorname{Im}w < 2\pi i \} \]
	\subsection{Отображение задаваемые функцией Жуковского}
	\[ f(z) = \frac{1}{2} (z + \frac{1}{z}) \]
	Найдем ее производную: $f'(z) = \dfrac{1}{2} (1 - \dfrac{1}{z^2})$. Производная не равна 0, при $z \neq \pm 1.$ \\ \noindent
	Очевидно, что $0 \mapsto \infty$ и $\infty \mapsto \infty$.
	 
	Рассмотрим $z_1 = 0$ и отображение $\dfrac{1}{f(z)}$
	\[ \frac{1}{f(z)} = \frac{2}{z + \frac{1}{z}} = \frac{2z}{z^2 + 1} = g(z) \Rightarrow g'(0) = 2 \Rightarrow w = f(z) \text{ конформно в точке } 0.\]
	
	Рассмотрим $z_2 = \infty$. Обозначим $s = \dfrac{1}{z}$. Тогда
	\[ h(s) = \frac{1}{2}(\frac{1}{s} + s) \Rightarrow h(s)\text{ конформно в точке } 0 \Rightarrow w = f(z) \text{ конформно в точке } \infty/ \]
	\textbf{Вывод:} отображение $ f(z) = \dfrac{1}{2} (z + \dfrac{1}{z}) $ конформно в каждой точке, кроме $ z = \pm 1 $
	\newpage
	\section{Лекция 12}
	\begin{statement}
		Функция Жуковского может быть записана как композиция двух следующих функций: 
		$w_1 = \dfrac{z - 1}{z + 1}$ и $w_2 = w_1^2$.
	\end{statement}
	\begin{proof}
		\[ w = \frac{1 + w_2}{1 - w_2} = \frac{1 + \left( \dfrac{z - 1}{z + 1}\right) ^2}{1 - \left( \dfrac{z - 1}{z + 1}\right) ^2} = \frac{2z^2 + 2}{4z} = \frac{1}{2}\left( z + \frac{1}{z}\right)  \]
	\end{proof}
	\begin{statement}
		Отображение $ f(z) = \frac{1}{2} (z + \frac{1}{z})$, конформно в области $ D_z $, если
		$ D_z $ одовременно не содержит точек $ z_1,\ z_2 : z_1z_2 = 1$ и $ \pm 1 \notin D_z.$
	\end{statement}
	\begin{proof}
		Исследуем на взаимооднозначность при $ z_1 \ne z_2. $
		\[w_1 - w_2 = \frac{1}{2}\left( z_1 + \frac{1}{z_1}\right)  - \frac{1}{2}\left( z_2 + \frac{1}{z_2}\right) = \frac{z_1-z_2}{2}\left( 1-\frac{1}{z_1z_2} \right) \Rightarrow w_1 \ne w_1 \iff z_1z_2 \ne 1 \]
	\end{proof}
	\subsection{Примеры}
	\noindent \textbf{1)} $ D_z = \{ z\in \Cm: |z| < R, R < 1 \} $\\
	Параметрически предстваляем границу: $ z = Re^{i\phi},\ -\pi < \phi \leqslant \pi$
	\[  w = \frac{1}{2}(Re^{i\phi} + \frac{1}{R}e^{-i\phi}) = \frac{1}{2}(R(\cos\phi + i\sin\phi) + \frac{1}{R}(\cos\phi - i\sin\phi)) \] 
	$ \begin{cases}
		u(R, \phi) = \dfrac{1}{2}\left( R+\dfrac{1}{R}\right)\cos\phi\\
		v(R, \phi) = \dfrac{1}{2}\left( R-\dfrac{1}{R}\right)\sin\phi
	\end{cases} $, геометрическое место этих точек --- эллипс.
	\[ \dfrac{u^2}{\dfrac{1}{2^2}\left(R +\dfrac{1}{R} \right)^2 } + \dfrac{v^2}{\dfrac{1}{2^2}\left( R-\dfrac{1}{R} \right)^2 } = 1 \]
	\[ D_w = \{ w \in \Cm: \frac{4(\operatorname{Re} w)^2}{\left( R+\dfrac{1}{R}\right) ^2} + \frac{4(\operatorname{Im} w)^2}{\left( R-\dfrac{1}{R}\right) ^2} > 1 \} \]
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\draw[fill=blue!20]
					(0,0) circle (0.75);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node at (1.1,-0.15) {$R<1$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}

			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5) % вся плоскость
					(0,0) ellipse (1.2 and 0.75); % луч (вычитается)
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (0,0) ellipse (1.2 and 0.75);
				\fill[black] (0,0.75) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$\frac{1}{2}(R-\frac{1}{R}) $};
				\fill[black] (1.2,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below left] {$\frac{1}{2}(R+\frac{1}{R}) $};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			% Стрелка между рисунками
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
			
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}

	\textbf{5)} $ D_z = \{ z\in\Cm: \operatorname{Im} > 0\} $\\
	Выполним анализ графика функции $ f(x) = \dfrac{1}{2}\left(x+\dfrac{1}{x}\right)  $
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1]
			\begin{scope}
				\begin{scope}
					\clip (-3,-3) rectangle (3,3);
					\draw[domain=-3:-0.1, smooth, variable=\x, blue, thick] 
					plot ({\x}, {0.5*(\x + 1/\x)});
					\draw[domain=0.1:3, smooth, variable=\x, blue, thick] 
					plot ({\x}, {0.5*(\x + 1/\x)});
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-3,0) -- (3,0) node[below] {$ x $};
				\draw[->] (0,-3) -- (0,3) node[below left] {$ y $};
				\draw[dashed] (1,0) -- (1,1);
				\draw[dashed] (0,1) -- (1,1);
				\draw[dashed] (-1,0) -- (-1,-1);
				\draw[dashed] (0,-1) -- (-1,-1);
				\fill (1,1) circle (1pt);
				\fill (-1,-1) circle (1pt);
				\node[below right] at (1,0) {$1$};
				\node[below left] at (0,1) {$1$};
				\node[below left] at (-1,0) {$-1$};
				\node[below right] at (0,-1) {$-1$};
			\end{scope}
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\begin{flalign*}
		&f' = \frac{1}{2}\left(1 - \frac{1}{x^2} \right) = 0 \Rightarrow x = \pm 1 \text{ экстремумы. }&\\
		&f'' = \frac{1}{x^2} \Rightarrow f''(1) = 1 > 0 \text{ --- выпукла вниз},\ f''(-1) = -1 > 0 \text{ --- выпукла вверх.}&
	\end{flalign*}
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
					(-1.5,-0.05) rectangle (-0.75,0.05)
					(0.75,0.05) rectangle (1.5,-0.05);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (-1.5,-0.05) rectangle (-0.75,0.05);
				\draw (0.75,0.05) rectangle (1.5,-0.05);
				\node[below left] at (0.75,0) {$1$};
				\node[below right] at (-0.75,0) {$-1$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
			
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\[ D_w = \Cm \setminus \{ w \in \Cm : \operatorname{Im} w = 0,\ \operatorname{Re} w \leqslant 0 \} \cup \{ w \in \Cm : \operatorname{Im} w = 0,\ \operatorname{Re} w \geqslant 0 \} \]
	\textbf{6)} $ D_z = \{ z\in\Cm: \operatorname{Im} < 0\} $\\

	\[ D_w = \Cm \setminus \{ w \in \Cm : \operatorname{Im} w = 0,\ \operatorname{Re} w \leqslant 0 \} \cup \{ w \in \Cm : \operatorname{Im} w = 0,\ \operatorname{Re} w \geqslant 0 \} \]
	\subsection{Отображение луночек и областей с разрывами}
	\begin{definition}
		\textbf{Луночка} --- область, граница которой имеет вид: $ \gamma_1 \cup \gamma_2 $, где  $ \gamma_1, \gamma_2 $ --- дуги обобщенных окружностей и
		$ \gamma_1 \cap \gamma_2 $ содержит две точки.
	\end{definition}
	\begin{example}
		Найти отображение, которое переводит $ D_z $ в $ D_w $, где\\ $ D_z = \{ z\in\Cm: |z| < 1,\ \operatorname{Im} > 0 \}, \ D_w = \{ w\in\Cm: \operatorname{Im} > 0 \}$
	\end{example}
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\draw[fill=blue!20] (-0.75,0) arc (180:0:0.75) -- cycle;
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\fill[black] (-0.75,0) circle (0.5pt) node[above left] {$-1$};
				\fill[black] (0.75,0) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$1$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]

				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			
			% Стрелка между рисунками

	Найдем отображение, которое переводит полуокружность в угол с центром в начале координат, для этого $ -1\mapsto 0 $ и $ 1\mapsto \infty $.\\

	Найдем, куда под действием отображения перейдут кривые:\\

	$ \Gamma_2: z = e^{i\phi},\ 0 \leqslant \phi \leqslant \pi$ перейдет в луч. ($ i \mapsto -i $)

	\begin{example}

	\[ z_1 =  -\frac{\sqrt 3}{2} + \frac{i}{2},\ z_2 = \frac{\sqrt 3}{2} + \frac{i}{2} \]
	Отображение $ w_1 = \dfrac{z - z_1}{z-z_2} $ такое, что $ z_1 \mapsto 0, \ z_2 \mapsto \infty,$ тогда \\
	$ 0 \mapsto \dfrac{z_1}{z_2} = \dfrac{-\sqrt 3 + i}{\sqrt 3 + i} = -\dfrac{1}{2} + \dfrac{\sqrt 3i}{2} $\\
	$ i \mapsto \dfrac{i - z_1}{i - z_2} = \dfrac{-\sqrt 3 + i}{\sqrt 3 + i} = -\dfrac{1}{2} - \dfrac{\sqrt 3i}{2} $
	\begin{center}

	В конце, отображением $ w = w^\frac{3}{2}_2 $ развернем угол.+7 917 835 16 19
	\begin{flalign*}
	&\text{Ответ: } w = -\left( \frac{2z+\sqrt 3 - i}{2z - \sqrt 3 - i}\right)^\frac{3}{2}&
	\end{flalign*}
	Общая схема:
	\begin{flalign*}
		&w_1 = \frac{z-z_1}{z-z_2}&\\
		&w_2 = e^{i\phi}w_1,\ \phi \in \R&\\
		&w = w_2^l,\ l \in \R&
	\end{flalign*}
	\begin{remark}
		$ z_1 $ и $ z_2 $ можно менять местами в выражении $ w_1 = \dfrac{z-z_2}{z-z_1} $
	\end{remark}
	\begin{example}
		Найти отображение, которое переводит $ D_z $ в $ D_w $, где\\ $ D_z = \Cm \setminus \{ z\in\Cm: \operatorname{Im}z = 0,\ x_1\leqslant\operatorname{Re}z \leqslant x_2 \}, \ D_w = \{ w\in\Cm: \operatorname{Im} > 0 \}$
	\end{example}
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
					(-0.5,-0.05) rectangle (0.75,0.05);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (-0.5,-0.05) rectangle (0.75,0.05);
				\node[above left] at (-0.5,0) {$x_1$};
				\node[above right] at (0.75,0) {$x_2$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
			
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Отобразим точку $ x_1 $ в $ 0 $, а точку $ x_2 $ в $ \infty $. Получим $ w_1 = \dfrac{z - x_1}{z - x_2} $.\\ Третью точку: $ \dfrac{x_1+x_2}{2} \mapsto -1 $.
	\newpage 
	Получится левый вырез, его повернем на $ \pi $ отображением: $ w_2 = e^{i\phi}w_1,\ \phi = \pi. $
	В конце, развернем угол в два раза отображением: $ w = w_2^\frac{1}{2}$.
	\begin{flalign*}
		&\text{Ответ: } w = \left( \frac{z - x_1}{x_2 - z}\right)^\frac{1}{2}&
	\end{flalign*}
	\newpage
	
	\section{Лекция 13}
	\subsection{Отображение луночки на верхнюю полуплоскость}
	\begin{example}
		Строим отображение луночки на верхнюю полуплоскость:
		\begin{center}
			\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					\begin{scope}
						\clip (-0.4,0) circle (1.4);
						\fill[blue!20] (0.4,0) circle (1.4);
					\end{scope}
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					% Границы луночки
					\draw (-0.4,0) ++(-90:1.4) arc[start angle=-90, end angle=90, radius=1.4];
					\draw (0.4,0) ++(270:1.4) arc[start angle=270, end angle=90, radius=1.4];
					
					% Точки пересечения (полюсы)
					\fill (0,{sqrt(1.4^2-0.4^2)}) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$z_1$};
					\fill (0,{-sqrt(1.4^2-0.4^2)}) circle (0.5pt) node[below right] {$z_2$};
					
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
		
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
				
			\end{tikzpicture}
		\end{center}
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item Для начала используем дробно-линейное отображение $w_1 = \dfrac{z - z_1}{z - z_2}$, где один из полюсов отправляем в 0, а другой в $\infty$
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\begin{scope}
							\clip (-0.4,0) circle (1.4);
							\fill[blue!20] (0.4,0) circle (1.4);
						\end{scope}
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						\draw (-0.4,0) ++(-90:1.4) arc[start angle=-90, end angle=90, radius=1.4];
						\draw (0.4,0) ++(270:1.4) arc[start angle=270, end angle=90, radius=1.4];
						
						\fill (0,{sqrt(1.4^2-0.4^2)}) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$z_1$};
						\fill (0,{-sqrt(1.4^2-0.4^2)}) circle (0.5pt) node[below right] {$z_2$};

						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
					\end{scope}
					
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) -- (20:1.3) arc[start angle=20, end angle=70, radius=1.3] -- cycle;
						
						% Оси
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						% Границы сектора
						\draw (0,0) -- (20:1.8);
						\draw (0,0) -- (70:1.8);
						\draw (20:1.8) arc[start angle=20, end angle=70, radius=1.8];
						
						% Обозначение 0 в вершине сектора
						\fill (0,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\draw (0.5,0) arc[start angle=0, end angle=20, radius=0.5];
						\node at (10:0.75) {$\alpha$};
						
						% Обозначение угла бета
						\draw (20:0.7) arc[start angle=20, end angle=70, radius=0.7];
						\node at (45:0.95) {$\beta$};
						
						% Подпись области
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$w_1$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			\newpage
			\item Далее при помощи $w_2 = e^{-i\alpha} w_1$ поворачиваем на угол $\alpha$ по часовой.
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
					% --- Область W1 (сектор до поворота) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						% Заливка сектора
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) -- (20:1.8) arc[start angle=20, end angle=70, radius=1.8] -- cycle;
						
						% Оси
						\draw[->] (-0.5,0) -- (2.0,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,2.0) node[above] {};
						
						% Границы сектора
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (20:1.8);
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (70:1.8);
						\draw[thick] (20:1.8) arc[start angle=20, end angle=70, radius=1.8];
						
						% Обозначение 0 в вершине сектора
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						% Обозначение угла альфа
						\draw[->] (0.5,0) arc[start angle=0, end angle=20, radius=0.5];
						\node at (10:0.75) {$\alpha$};
						
						% Обозначение угла бета
						\draw[->] (20:0.7) arc[start angle=20, end angle=70, radius=0.7];
						\node at (45:0.95) {$\beta$};
						
						% Подпись области
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.1,1.2) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W2 (повёрнутый сектор) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4cm]
						% Заливка повёрнутого сектора (теперь от 0 до бета)
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) -- (0:1.8) arc[start angle=0, end angle=50, radius=1.8] -- cycle;
						
						% Оси
						\draw[->] (-0.5,0) -- (2.0,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,2.0) node[above] {};
						
						% Границы сектора
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0:1.8);
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (50:1.8);
						\draw[thick] (0:1.8) arc[start angle=0, end angle=50, radius=1.8];
						
						% Обозначение 0 в вершине сектора
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						% Обозначение угла бета
						\draw[->] (0.5,0) arc[start angle=0, end angle=50, radius=0.5];
						\node at (25:0.75) {$\beta$};
						
						% Подпись области
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (0.9,0.8) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_2 = e^{-i\alpha} w_1$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			\item На последнем шаге нужно раскрыть наш сектор из угла $\beta$ до угла $\pi$, используя отображение $w = w_2^{\frac{\pi}{\beta}}$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
					% --- Область W2 (сектор от 0 до бета) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						% Заливка сектора
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) -- (0:1.8) arc[start angle=0, end angle=50, radius=1.8] -- cycle;
						
						% Оси
						\draw[->] (-0.5,0) -- (2.0,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,2.0) node[above] {};
						
						% Границы сектора
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0:1.8);
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (50:1.8);
						\draw[thick] (0:1.8) arc[start angle=0, end angle=50, radius=1.8];
						
						% Обозначение 0 в вершине сектора
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						% Обозначение угла бета
						\draw[->] (0.5,0) arc[start angle=0, end angle=50, radius=0.5];
						\node at (25:0.75) {$\beta$};
						
						% Подпись области
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (0.9,0.8) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W (верхняя полуплоскость) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						% Обозначение 0
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						% Подпись области
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.05cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w = w_2^{\pi/\beta}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
		\end{enumerate}
	\end{example}
	\subsection{Отображение плоскости с выколотым отрезком на верхнюю полуплоскость}
	\begin{example}
		Строим отображение плоскости с выколотым отрезком $[z_1, z_2]$ на верхнюю полуплоскость:
		\begin{center}
			\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
				% --- Область Z (плоскость с выколотым отрезком) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					% Заливка всей плоскости
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.5) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
					
					% Оси
					\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					% Выколотый отрезок
					\draw[white, line width=6pt] (-0.6,0.8) -- (0.8,-0.4);
					\draw[thick] (-0.62,0.82) -- (0.78,-0.38);
					\draw[thick] (-0.58,0.78) -- (0.82,-0.42);
					
					% Концы отрезка
					\fill[red] (-0.6,0.8) circle (1.2pt) node[above left] {$z_1$};
					\fill[red] (0.8,-0.4) circle (1.2pt) node[below right] {$z_2$};
					
					% Середина отрезка
					\fill[blue] (0.1,0.2) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$\frac{z_1+z_2}{2}$};
					
					% Подпись области
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.9) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Область W (верхняя полуплоскость) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					% Обозначение 0
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					% Подпись области
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Стрелка ---
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above] {$f$};
				
			\end{tikzpicture}
		\end{center}
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item Используем дробно-линейное отображение $w_1 = \frac{z - z_1}{z - z_2}$. Отрезок $[z_1, z_2]$ переходит в луч. Проверим середину отрезка:
			\[
			\frac{z_1 + z_2}{2} \xrightarrow{w_1} \frac{\frac{z_1+z_2}{2} - z_1}{\frac{z_1+z_2}{2} - z_2} = \frac{z_2 - z_1}{z_1 - z_2} = -1
			\]
			Значит, отрезок переходит в луч $(-\infty, 0]$.
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область Z ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.5) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (-0.6,0.8) -- (0.8,-0.4);
						\draw[thick] (-0.62,0.82) -- (0.78,-0.38);
						\draw[thick] (-0.58,0.78) -- (0.82,-0.42);
						\fill[red] (-0.6,0.8) circle (1.2pt) node[above left] {$z_1$};
						\fill[red] (0.8,-0.4) circle (1.2pt) node[below right] {$z_2$};
						\fill[blue] (0.1,0.2) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$\frac{z_1+z_2}{2}$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.9) {$z$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W1 (плоскость с выколотым лучом) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.5) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						% Выколотый луч (-∞, 0]
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (-1.8,0) -- (0,0);
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,0.05) -- (0,0.05);
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,-0.05) -- (0,-0.05);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[blue] (-1,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$-1$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,1.0) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_1 = \frac{z-z_1}{z-z_2}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Разворачиваем луч при помощи $w_2 = e^{i\pi} w_1 = -w_1$. Луч $(-\infty, 0]$ переходит в $[0, +\infty)$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.5) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (-1.8,0) -- (0,0);
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,0.05) -- (0,0.05);
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,-0.05) -- (0,-0.05);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[blue] (-1,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$-1$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,1.0) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W2 (луч [0, +∞)) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.5) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						% Выколотый луч [0, +∞)
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (1.8,0);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.05) -- (1.8,0.05);
						\draw[thick] (0,-0.05) -- (1.8,-0.05);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[blue] (1,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$1$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.0) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_2 = -w_1$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Наконец, извлекаем корень $w = w_2^{1/2}$. Луч $[0, +\infty)$ раскрывается в верхнюю полуплоскость:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.5) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (1.8,0);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.05) -- (1.8,0.05);
						\draw[thick] (0,-0.05) -- (1.8,-0.05);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[blue] (1,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$1$};
						
						% Обозначение берегов разреза
						\node[above right] at (0.8,0.15) {$w_2 = r e^{i0}$};
						\node[below right] at (0.8,-0.15) {$w_2 = r e^{i2\pi}$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.0) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W (верхняя полуплоскость) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w = w_2^{1/2}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
		\end{enumerate}
		\textbf{Ответ:} $w = \sqrt{\frac{z-z_1}{z_2-z}}$
	\end{example}
	
	\newpage
	\subsection{Отображение верхней полуплоскости с вертикальным разрезом на верхнюю полуплоскость}
	\begin{example}
		Строим отображение верхней полуплоскости с вертикальным разрезом на верхнюю полуплоскость:
		\begin{center}
			\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
				% --- Область Z (верхняя полуплоскость с разрезом от 0 до ih) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					% Заливка верхней полуплоскости
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
					
					% Оси
					\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					% Вертикальный разрез от 0 до ih
					\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.6);
					\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.6);
					\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.6);
					
					% Точка ih
					\fill[red] (0,0.6) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ih$};
					
					% Обозначение 0
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					% Подпись области
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.0) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Область W (верхняя полуплоскость) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					% Обозначение 0
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					% Подпись области
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Стрелка ---
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above] {$f$};
				
			\end{tikzpicture}
		\end{center}
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item Первым шагом возводим в квадрат: $w_1 = z^2$. Верхняя полуплоскость переходит в плоскость с разрезом вдоль горизонтальной оси. Вертикальный разрез $[0, ih]$ переходит в горизонтальный $[-h^2, +\infty)$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область Z ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.6);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.6);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.6);
						\fill[red] (0,0.6) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ih$};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.0) {$z$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.5) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						% Разрез [-h^2, +∞)
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (-0.8,0) -- (1.8,0);
						\draw[thick] (-0.8,0.05) -- (1.8,0.05);
						\draw[thick] (-0.8,-0.05) -- (1.8,-0.05);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (-0.8,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$-h^2$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.0) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_1 = z^2$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Сдвигаем разрез: $w_2 = w_1 + h^2$. Разрез $[-h^2, +\infty)$ переходит в $[0, +\infty)$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.5) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (-0.8,0) -- (1.8,0);
						\draw[thick] (-0.8,0.05) -- (1.8,0.05);
						\draw[thick] (-0.8,-0.05) -- (1.8,-0.05);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (-0.8,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$-h^2$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.0) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.5) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						% Разрез [0, +∞)
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (1.8,0);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.05) -- (1.8,0.05);
						\draw[thick] (0,-0.05) -- (1.8,-0.05);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.0) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_2 = w_1 + h^2$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Наконец, извлекаем корень $w = w_2^{1/2}$. Угол $2\pi$ сворачивается в верхнюю полуплоскость:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.5) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (1.8,0);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.05) -- (1.8,0.05);
						\draw[thick] (0,-0.05) -- (1.8,-0.05);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						% Обозначение берегов разреза
						\node[above right] at (0.8,0.15) {$w_2 = r e^{i0}$};
						\node[below right] at (0.8,-0.15) {$w_2 = r e^{i2\pi}$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.0) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w = w_2^{1/2}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
		\end{enumerate}
		\textbf{Ответ:} $w = \sqrt{z^2 + h^2}$
	\end{example}
	\subsection{Отображение полоски с вертикальным разрезом на верхнюю полуплоскость}
	\begin{example}
		Строим отображение верхней полуплоскости с вертикальным разрезом $[0, ih]$ и ограничением $i\alpha$ ($\alpha > h$) на верхнюю полуплоскость:
		\begin{center}
			\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
				% --- Область Z ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					% Заливка полосы
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
					
					% Оси
					\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					% Верхняя граница i\alpha
					\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
					\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$i\alpha$};
					
					% Вертикальный разрез от 0 до ih
					\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.5);
					\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.5);
					\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.5);
					
					% Точка ih
					\fill[red] (0,0.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ih$};
					
					% Обозначение 0
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					% Подпись области
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.8) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Область W ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Стрелка ---
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above] {$f$};
				
			\end{tikzpicture}
		\end{center}
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item Растягиваем полосу: $w_1 = z \cdot \frac{\pi}{\alpha}$. Получаем полосу высоты $\pi$ с разрезом от $0$ до $ic$, где $c = \frac{\pi h}{\alpha}$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область Z ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$i\alpha$};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.5);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.5);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.5);
						\fill[red] (0,0.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ih$};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.8) {$z$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						
						% Верхняя граница i\pi
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.5) -- (1.8,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						
						% Разрез от 0 до ic
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.7);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,0.7) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ic$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,1.2) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_1 = \frac{\pi}{\alpha} z$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Применяем экспоненту: $w_2 = e^{w_1}$. Полоса переходит в верхнюю полуплоскость с разрезом по дуге окружности от $1$ до $e^{ic}$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (-1.5,1.5) -- (1.5,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.7);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,0.7) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ic$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,1.2) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						% Верхняя полуплоскость с вырезанным сектором
						\begin{scope}
							\clip (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							% Вырезаем сектор (белая область)
							\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[white] (0,0) -- (1.3,0) arc[start angle=0, end angle=55, radius=1.3] -- cycle;
						\end{scope}
						
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						
						% Границы разреза (две дуги)
						\draw[thick] (1.3,0) arc[start angle=0, end angle=55, radius=1.3];
						\draw[thick] (1.3,0.05) arc[start angle=1, end angle=54, radius=1.3];
						\draw[thick] (1.3,-0.05) arc[start angle=-1, end angle=52, radius=1.3];
						
						% Радиальные линии от 0 до дуги (границы сектора)
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (1.3,0);
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (1.3*0.574,1.3*0.819);
						
						% Единичная окружность (пунктиром)
						\draw[gray, dashed] (0,0) circle (1.3);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (1.3,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below right] {$1$};
						\fill[red] (1.3*0.574,1.3*0.819) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$e^{ic}$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_2 = e^{w_1}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Дробно-линейное отображение $w_3 = \frac{w_2 - 1}{w_2 + 1}$ переводит разрез в вертикальный отрезок $[0, i\tan\frac{c}{2}]$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\begin{scope}
							\clip (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[white] (0,0) -- (1.3,0) arc[start angle=0, end angle=55, radius=1.3] -- cycle;
						\end{scope}
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (1.3,0) arc[start angle=0, end angle=55, radius=1.3];
						\draw[thick] (1.3,0.05) arc[start angle=1, end angle=54, radius=1.3];
						\draw[thick] (1.3,-0.05) arc[start angle=-1, end angle=52, radius=1.3];
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (1.3,0);
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (1.3*0.574,1.3*0.819);
						\draw[gray, dashed] (0,0) circle (1.3);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (1.3,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below right] {$1$};
						\fill[red] (1.3*0.574,1.3*0.819) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$e^{ic}$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W3 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						% Вертикальный разрез (белая полоса с границами)
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.65);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.65);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.65);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,0.65) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i\tan\frac{c}{2}$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,1.0) {$w_3$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_3 = \frac{w_2-1}{w_2+1}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Сводим к предыдущей задаче: $w = \sqrt{w_3^2 + \tan^2\frac{c}{2}}$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W3 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.6);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.6);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.6);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,0.6) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i\tan\frac{c}{2}$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,1.0) {$w_3$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w = \sqrt{w_3^2 + \tan^2\frac{c}{2}}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
		\end{enumerate}
		\textbf{Ответ:} $w = \sqrt{\left(\frac{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} - 1}{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} + 1}\right)^2 + \tan^2\frac{c}{2}}$, где $c = \frac{\pi h}{\alpha}$.
	\end{example}
	\newpage
	\subsection{Отображение полоски с вертикальным разрезом на полоску}
	\begin{example}
		Строим отображение полосы высоты $\alpha$ с вертикальным разрезом $[0, ih]$ на полосу высоты $\alpha$ без разреза:
		\begin{center}
			\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
				% --- Область Z (полоса с разрезом) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					% Заливка полосы
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
					
					% Оси
					\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					% Верхняя граница i\alpha
					\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
					\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$i\alpha$};
					
					% Вертикальный разрез от 0 до ih
					\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.5);
					\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.5);
					\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.5);
					
					% Точка ih
					\fill[red] (0,0.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ih$};
					
					% Обозначение 0
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					% Подпись области
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.8) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Область W (полоса без разреза) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
					\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
					\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$i\alpha$};
					
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.8) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Стрелка ---
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above] {$w$};
				
			\end{tikzpicture}
		\end{center}
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item Используем результат предыдущей задачи: $w_1 = \sqrt{\left(\frac{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} - 1}{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} + 1}\right)^2 + \tan^2\frac{c}{2}}$, где $c = \frac{\pi h}{\alpha}$. Это отображение переводит полосу с разрезом в верхнюю полуплоскость:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область Z ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$i\alpha$};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.5);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.5);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.5);
						\fill[red] (0,0.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ih$};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.8) {$z$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W1 (верхняя полуплоскость) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above, font=\footnotesize] {$w_1 = \sqrt{\left(\frac{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} - 1}{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} + 1}\right)^2 + \tan^2\frac{c}{2}}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Логарифмируем: $w_2 = \ln w_1$. Верхняя полуплоскость переходит в полосу высоты $\pi$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W2 (полоса высоты \pi) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.5) -- (1.8,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_2 = \ln w_1$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Сжимаем полосу обратно: $w = \frac{\alpha}{\pi} w_2$. Получаем полосу высоты $\alpha$ без разреза:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.5) -- (1.8,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W (полоса высоты \alpha) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$i\alpha$};
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.8) {$w$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w = \frac{\alpha}{\pi} w_2$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
		\end{enumerate}
		\textbf{Ответ:} $w = \frac{\alpha}{\pi} \ln \sqrt{\left(\frac{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} - 1}{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} + 1}\right)^2 + \tan^2\frac{c}{2}}$, где $c = \frac{\pi h}{\alpha}$.
	\end{example}
	\subsection{Отображение полуполосы с горизонтальным на разрезом на верхнюю полуплоскость}
	\begin{example}
		Строим отображение полуполосы $\{z: \operatorname{Re}z > 0, 0 < \operatorname{Im}z < h\}$ с горизонтальным разрезом $[0, \alpha]$ на высоте $\frac{ih}{2}$ на верхнюю полуплоскость:
		\begin{center}
			\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
				% --- Область Z (полуполоса с разрезом) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					% Заливка полуполосы
					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
					
					% Оси
					\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					% Левая граница (Re z = 0)
					\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.2);
					
					% Верхняя граница
					\draw[thick] (0,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
					\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$ih$};
					
					% Горизонтальный разрез на высоте ih/2
					\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0.6) -- (0.8,0.6);
					\draw[thick] (0,0.58) -- (0.8,0.58);
					\draw[thick] (0,0.62) -- (0.8,0.62);
					
					% Конец разреза
					\fill[red] (0.8,0.6) circle (1.2pt) node[above] {$\alpha$};
					
					% Обозначение 0
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					% Подпись области
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,0.9) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Область W (верхняя полуплоскость) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Стрелка ---
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above] {$f$};
				
			\end{tikzpicture}
		\end{center}
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item Растягиваем: $w_1 = z \cdot \frac{\pi}{h}$. Получаем полуполосу высоты $\pi$ с разрезом от $0$ до $c = \frac{\pi \alpha}{h}$ на высоте $\frac{i\pi}{2}$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область Z ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.2);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$ih$};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0.6) -- (0.8,0.6);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.58) -- (0.8,0.58);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.62) -- (0.8,0.62);
						\fill[red] (0.8,0.6) circle (1.2pt) node[above] {$\alpha$};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,0.9) {$z$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.5) -- (1.8,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						
						% Разрез на высоте i\pi/2
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0.75) -- (1.0,0.75);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.73) -- (1.0,0.73);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.77) -- (1.0,0.77);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (1.0,0.75) circle (1.2pt) node[above] {$c$};
						
						\node at (0,0.75) [left] {$\frac{i\pi}{2}$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,1.2) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_1 = \frac{\pi}{h} z$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Экспонента: $w_2 = e^{w_1}$. Полуполоса переходит во внешность единичной полуокружности с вертикальным разрезом от $i$ до $ie^c$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.5) -- (1.5,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0.75) -- (1.0,0.75);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.73) -- (1.0,0.73);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.77) -- (1.0,0.77);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (1.0,0.75) circle (1.2pt) node[above] {$c$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,1.2) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W2 (внешность полуокружности с вертикальным разрезом) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\begin{scope}
							\clip (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							% Вырезаем нижний полукруг (единичная полуокружность)
							\fill[white] (0,0) circle (1.0);
							% Вырезаем вертикальный разрез от i до i e^C
							\fill[white] (-0.05,1.0) rectangle (0.05,1.5);
						\end{scope}
						
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						
						% Единичная полуокружность
						\draw[thick] (0,0) circle (1.0);
						
						% Вертикальный разрез от i до i e^C
						\draw[thick] (0,1.0) -- (0,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,1.0) -- (-0.05,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,1.0) -- (0.05,1.5);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,1.0) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i$};
						\fill[red] (0,1.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ie^c$};
						
						% Точки -1 и 1 на вещественной оси
						\fill[black] (-1.0,0) circle (0.8pt) node[below] {$-1$};
						\fill[black] (1.0,0) circle (0.8pt) node[below] {$1$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_2 = e^{w_1}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Функция Жуковского: $w_3 = \frac{1}{2}\left(w_2 + \frac{1}{w_2}\right)$. Внешность полуокружности с разрезом переходит в верхнюю полуплоскость с вертикальным разрезом $[0, i\sh c]$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\begin{scope}
							\clip (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[white] (0,0) circle (1.0);
							\fill[white] (-0.05,1.0) rectangle (0.05,1.5);
						\end{scope}
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (0,0) circle (1.0);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.0) -- (0,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,1.0) -- (-0.05,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,1.0) -- (0.05,1.5);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,1.0) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i$};
						\fill[red] (0,1.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ie^c$};
						\fill[black] (-1.0,0) circle (0.8pt) node[below] {$-1$};
						\fill[black] (1.0,0) circle (0.8pt) node[below] {$1$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W3 (верхняя полуплоскость с вертикальным разрезом) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						% Вертикальный разрез от 0 до i sh C
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.7);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,0.7) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i\sh c$};
						
						% Точки -1 и 1 на вещественной оси
						\fill[black] (-1.0,0) circle (0.8pt) node[below] {$-1$};
						\fill[black] (1.0,0) circle (0.8pt) node[below] {$1$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,1.0) {$w_3$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_3 = \frac{1}{2}\left(w_2 + \frac{1}{w_2}\right)$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Используем результат предыдущей задачи: $w = \sqrt{w_3^2 + \sh^2 c}$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W3 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.7);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,0.7) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i\sh c$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,1.0) {$w_3$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w = \sqrt{w_3^2 + \sh^2 c}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
		\end{enumerate}
		\textbf{Ответ:} $w = \sqrt{\ch^2\left(\frac{\pi z}{h}\right) + \sh^2 c}$, где $c = \frac{\pi \alpha}{h}$.
	\end{example}
	\subsection{Отображение полуполосы с горизонтальным разрезом на полуполосу без разреза}
	\begin{example}
		Строим отображение полуполосы $\{z: \operatorname{Re}z > 0, 0 < \operatorname{Im}z < h\}$ с горизонтальным разрезом $[0, \alpha]$ на высоте $\frac{ih}{2}$ на полуполосу без разреза:
		\begin{center}
			\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
				% --- Область Z (полуполоса с разрезом) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					% Заливка полуполосы
					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
					
					% Оси
					\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					% Левая граница (Re z = 0)
					\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.2);
					
					% Верхняя граница
					\draw[thick] (0,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
					\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$ih$};
					
					% Горизонтальный разрез на высоте ih/2
					\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0.6) -- (0.8,0.6);
					\draw[thick] (0,0.58) -- (0.8,0.58);
					\draw[thick] (0,0.62) -- (0.8,0.62);
					
					% Конец разреза
					\fill[red] (0.8,0.6) circle (1.2pt) node[above] {$\alpha$};
					
					% Обозначение 0
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					% Подпись области
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,0.9) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Область W (полуполоса без разреза) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
					\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.2);
					\draw[thick] (0,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
					\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$ih$};
					
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,0.9) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Стрелка ---
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above] {$f$};
				
			\end{tikzpicture}
		\end{center} 
		\newpage
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item Используем результат предыдущей задачи: $w_1 = \sqrt{\ch^2\left(\frac{\pi z}{h}\right) + \sh^2 c}$, где $c = \frac{\pi \alpha}{h}$. Это отображение переводит полуполосу с разрезом в верхнюю полуплоскость:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область Z ---
